				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					La Didone abbandonata (Hasse, Johann Adolph)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 Acts (each with 19, 16, 21 scenes)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">La Didone abbandonata
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Dramma per musica in  tre atti
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Hasse,_Johann_Adolph" title="Category:Hasse, Johann Adolph">Hasse, Johann Adolph</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJH 36
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 Acts (each with 19, 16, 21 scenes)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1742-10-07 in Hubertusburg: Court Theatre <span style="background:#c2c8cd;color:#003d70;padding:0 4px">A</span><br />1743-02-04 in Dresden: Hofoper (<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:Opernhaus_am_Zwinger" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:en:Opernhaus am Zwinger">Opernhaus am Zwinger</a>) <span style="background:#c2c8cd;color:#003d70;padding:0 4px">B</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Algarotti,_Francesco" title="Category:Algarotti, Francesco">Francesco Algarotti</a>, after <a href="/wiki/Category:Metastasio,_Pietro" title="Category:Metastasio, Pietro">Pietro Metastasio</a> (1698-1782)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>Italian
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Average Duration</span><span class="ms555">Avg. Duration</span>
</th>
<td>2 3/4 hours
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque" title="Category:Baroque">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque_style" title="Category:Baroque style">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td><i>Voices:</i> 4 sopranos, alto, bass; mixed chorus (SATB)<br /><i>Orchestra:</i> 2 flutes, 2 oboes, 2 horns, strings, continuo
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>External Links
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.allmusic.com/composition/didone-abbandonata-opera-mc0002686172">All Music Guide</a></span><br /><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://opac.rism.info/metaopac/search?q=rism469108700&amp;db=251&amp;View=rism&amp;Language=en">FS manuscript copy (D-Bsa SA 1087)</a></span>
</td></tr></table>
